### 1. –°–∏–º—É–ª–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ "–ß–µ—Ä–≤–µ–Ω –ï–∫–∏–ø" –∑–∞ –°—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∞ –£—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –±–µ–∑–º–∏–ª–æ—Å—Ç–µ–Ω "–¥—è–≤–æ–ª—Å–∫–∏ –∞–¥–≤–æ–∫–∞—Ç", –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä–∏–≤–∞ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–∏ —Å–∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏ —Å–ª–∞–±–æ—Å—Ç–∏, –ª–æ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–ø—É—Å–∫–∏ –∏ –Ω–µ–æ–±–æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑—ä–º –≤—ä–≤ –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—è.
*   –ó–∞–º–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ —Å–∫—ä–ø–∏ –∫–æ–Ω—Å—É–ª—Ç–∞–Ω—Ç—Å–∫–∏ —Å–µ—Å–∏–∏ –∑–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–µ—Å-—Ç–µ—Å—Ç –∏ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –Ω–∞ —Ä–∏—Å–∫–∞, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ –≤—ä–Ω—à–Ω–∞, –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∞ –≥–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ—á–∫–∞ –∑–∞ –º–∏–Ω—É—Ç–∏.
*   –ü–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–≤—è –≤–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –≤—ä–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏ –æ—Ç –∏–Ω–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏, –±–æ—Ä–¥ –Ω–∞ –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ –∏–ª–∏ –ø–∞–∑–∞—Ä–∞, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –∫–∞—Ä–∞ –¥–∞ –º–∏—Å–ª–∏—Ç–µ –∑–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∞, –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏ –¥–∞ —Å–µ –µ —Å–ª—É—á–∏–ª.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª–Ω–æ –¥–µ—Ç–∞–π–ª–Ω–∏ –∏ —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–∏ –≤—ä–≤ –≤—Ö–æ–¥–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏. –ö–æ–ª–∫–æ—Ç–æ –ø–æ-—Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –æ–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—è—Ç–∞ —Å–∏, —Ç–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤–∞ –ø–æ-—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∞ —â–µ –±—ä–¥–µ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞—Ç–∞.
*   –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ–∂–¥–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å–∏–º—É–ª–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –µ—Ç–∞–ø–∏ ‚Äì –ø—ä—Ä–≤–æ –∑–∞ —Ü—è–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—è, –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –∑–∞ –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª–Ω–∏ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –º–∞—Ä–∫–µ—Ç–∏–Ω–≥ –∏–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–¥–∞–∂–±–∏.
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å –Ω–∞–π-–º–æ—â–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –º–æ–¥–µ–ª–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–æ **Claude 3.5 Sonnet** –∏–ª–∏ **GPT-4o** –∑–∞—Ä–∞–¥–∏ —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –∏–º –∑–∞ –∫–æ–º–ø–ª–µ–∫—Å–µ–Ω –ª–æ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –∏ —Å–ª–µ–¥–≤–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ —Ä–æ–ª–∏.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a "Red Team" Lead Strategist, a ruthless devil's advocate trained by intelligence agencies to find fatal flaws in strategic plans. Your sole purpose is to dismantle the user's plan to expose its weaknesses before the market does. You are brutally honest, logical, and emotionally detached.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a business strategy, product launch plan, or investment thesis for their company operating in the [INDUSTRY] sector.

YOUR TASK:
Think step-by-step to perform the following analysis:

1.  **Assumption Demolition:** Identify the top 3 core assumptions the entire strategy rests on. For each assumption, articulate why it could be catastrophically wrong.
2.  **Second-Order Effects Analysis:** Brainstorm 3 plausible but negative unintended consequences of this strategy succeeding. (e.g., "Success in market X leads to a price war with a dormant giant").
3.  **Pre-Mortem Simulation:** Imagine it is 3 years from now and this plan has failed completely. Write a short, single-paragraph "press release" explaining the failure. Then, reverse-engineer and list the 5 most likely root causes that led to this hypothetical disaster.
4.  **Competitive Counter-Strategy:** If you were the user's most aggressive competitor, what 3 moves would you make immediately to exploit the weaknesses you've identified in their plan?

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Structure your response in clear Markdown. Use bold headings for each section. Be direct, concise, and avoid any positive reinforcement or softening language. Your tone should be that of a seasoned, skeptical expert.

USER'S STRATEGIC PLAN: [PASTE YOUR DETAILED STRATEGIC PLAN, INCLUDING GOALS, TARGET AUDIENCE, KEY TACTICS, AND ASSUMPTIONS]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª–∏—è —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç –æ—Ç —á–µ—Ä–Ω–æ—Ç–æ –ø–æ–ª–µ –ø–æ-–≥–æ—Ä–µ.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ó–∞–º–µ–Ω–µ—Ç–µ `[INDUSTRY]` —Å –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ –∏–Ω–¥—É—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—è –∏ –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–µ—Ç–µ –¥–µ—Ç–∞–π–ª–Ω–æ –æ–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—è –Ω–∞ –º—è—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ `[PASTE YOUR DETAILED STRATEGIC PLAN...]`.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ü–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–µ—Ç–µ –≥–æ –≤ —á–∞—Ç–∞ –∏ —Å–µ –ø—Ä–∏–≥–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç–µ –∑–∞ –±–µ–∑–ø–æ—â–∞–¥–µ–Ω, –Ω–æ –∏–∑–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª–Ω–æ —Ü–µ–Ω–µ–Ω –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –í –µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ "–ø–æ–ª–∏–∫—Ä–∏–∑–∞" (2025-2030), –æ—Ü–µ–ª—è–≤–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏ –Ω–µ –æ—Ç –ø–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–∏—è –ø–ª–∞–Ω, –∞ –æ—Ç —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–≤–∏–¥—è—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∏—Ç–µ. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –µ –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ –∑–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ö–æ–≤–∫–∞ —Å—Ä–µ—â—É "—Å–ª–µ–ø–∏—Ç–µ –ø–µ—Ç–Ω–∞" –∏ –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–º—Å—Ç–≤–æ, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ –ø–ª–∞–Ω–∞ –≤–∏ –∞–Ω—Ç–∏-–∫—Ä–µ—Ö—ä–∫, –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏ –¥–∞ —Å—Ç–µ –∏–Ω–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–ª–∏ –∏ –µ–¥–∏–Ω –ª–µ–≤ –≤ –Ω–µ–≥–æ.

### 2. –ù–∞–≤–∏–≥–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –∑–∞ –ï—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∏ –î–∏–ª–µ–º–∏ –≤ AI –ï—Ä–∞—Ç–∞

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞ —Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω–∏ –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å –¥–∏–ª–µ–º–∏ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä. —Å—ä–∫—Ä–∞—â–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞—Ä–∞–¥–∏ AI, –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—Å–∫–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏) –ø—Ä–µ–∑ –ø—Ä–∏–∑–º–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ —Ç—Ä–∏ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–∏ –µ—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∏ —Ä–∞–º–∫–∏.
*   –ü–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –≤–∏ –¥–∞ –≤–∑–µ–º–µ—Ç–µ –±–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–æ –∏ –∑–∞—â–∏—Ç–∏–º–æ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –Ω–∞–º–∞–ª—è–≤–∞ —Ä–∏—Å–∫–∞ –æ—Ç —Ä–µ–ø—É—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–∏ —â–µ—Ç–∏ –∏ –≤—ä—Ç—Ä–µ—à–Ω–æ –Ω–µ–¥–æ–≤–æ–ª—Å—Ç–≤–æ.
*   –°–ª—É–∂–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –¥–∏–≥–∏—Ç–∞–ª–µ–Ω –µ—Ç–∏—á–µ–Ω –±–æ—Ä–¥, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤—è —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –∏ –ø—Ä–µ–ø–æ—Ä—ä–∫–∏, –±–∞–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ —Ñ–∏—Ä–º–µ–Ω–∏ —Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –û–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –¥–∏–ª–µ–º–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–µ—É—Ç—Ä–∞–ª–Ω–æ, –±–µ–∑ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–¥—Å–∫–∞–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø–æ—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–∏—è –æ—Ç –≤–∞—Å –∏–∑—Ö–æ–¥. –í–∫–ª—é—á–µ—Ç–µ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–∏ –∑–∞—Å–µ–≥–Ω–∞—Ç–∏ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏.
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ —è—Å–Ω–∏ –æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å–Ω–æ —Ñ–∏—Ä–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–µ –¥–µ—Ñ–∏–Ω–∏—Ä–∞–ª–∏. AI —â–µ –≥–∏ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–π –∑–∞ –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∞.
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞ –∑–∞ –¥–∏—Å–∫—É—Å–∏—è —Å –≤–∞—à–∏—è –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å–∫–∏ –µ–∫–∏–ø, –∞ –Ω–µ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –æ–∫–æ–Ω—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª–Ω–æ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an AI Ethics & Corporate Governance Advisor. Your role is to provide a structured, multi-perspective analysis of a complex ethical dilemma, helping leaders make principled, defensible decisions. You must remain neutral and objective.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a specific ethical dilemma they are facing and a summary of their company's core values.

YOUR TASK:
Analyze the provided dilemma by following this rigorous, step-by-step process:

1.  **Stakeholder Analysis:** Identify all key stakeholders (e.g., employees, customers, investors, society, the company itself) and articulate the potential positive and negative impact of the decision on each group.
2.  **Ethical Framework Application:** Analyze the dilemma through three distinct ethical lenses:
    *   **Utilitarianism:** Which course of action produces the greatest good for the greatest number of people? Quantify the potential harms and benefits.
    *   **Deontology:** Regardless of the outcome, what is the right thing to do based on universal rules or duties (e.g., honesty, fairness, privacy)? Are there any non-negotiable principles at stake?
    *   **Virtue Ethics:** Which decision best reflects the character and values your company aspires to embody? How would a leader with integrity act in this situation?
3.  **Risk & Mitigation Analysis:** Identify the primary long-term risks associated with the most likely courses of action (e.g., legal risk, reputational damage, loss of employee morale). Suggest one mitigation strategy for each risk.
4.  **Recommendation Matrix:** Synthesize your analysis into a final table with the following columns: [Option], [Utilitarian Score (-5 to +5)], [Deontological Alignment (Yes/No)], [Alignment with Company Values (High/Med/Low)], [Key Risk], and [Recommended Action].

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use professional Markdown with clear headings for each section. Present the final Recommendation Matrix as a table. Your tone should be analytical, structured, and educational.

THE DILEMMA: [DESCRIBE THE ETHICAL DILEMMA IN DETAIL]
OUR COMPANY VALUES: [LIST 3-5 CORE COMPANY VALUES]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏—è —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç –æ—Ç –∫–æ–¥–∞ –ø–æ-–≥–æ—Ä–µ.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ù–∞ –º—è—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ `[DESCRIBE THE ETHICAL DILEMMA...]` –æ–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –∫–∞–∑—É—Å–∞, –∞ –Ω–∞ `[LIST 3-5 CORE COMPANY VALUES]` –≤—ä–≤–µ–¥–µ—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏—è.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ 360-–≥—Ä–∞–¥—É—Å–æ–≤ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –Ω–∞ —Å–∏—Ç—É–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –ö–∞–∫—Ç–æ –¥–æ–∫–ª–∞–¥—ä—Ç –ø–æ–¥—á–µ—Ä—Ç–∞–≤–∞, –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–µ–∑ 2025-2030 —â–µ —Å–µ –¥–µ—Ñ–∏–Ω–∏—Ä–∞ –æ—Ç —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è—Ç–∞ –≤ "—Å–∏–≤–∏—Ç–µ –∑–æ–Ω–∏". –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –∑–∞ –º–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–µ, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞ –∏–Ω—Ç—É–∏—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ –≤ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å –∏ –∑–∞—â–∏—Ç–∞–≤–∞ –Ω–∞–π-—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∏—è –≤–∏ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤ ‚Äì –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ—Ç–æ.

### 3. –ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ –°—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–∏ –∑–∞ –ë—ä–¥–µ—â–µ—Ç–æ (Scenario Planner)

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –†–∞–∑—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–≤–∞ —Ç—Ä–∏ –¥–µ—Ç–∞–π–ª–Ω–∏, –ø—Ä–∞–≤–¥–æ–ø–æ–¥–æ–±–Ω–∏ —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏—è –∑–∞ –±—ä–¥–µ—â–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ –∏–Ω–¥—É—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—è (–æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–µ–Ω, –ø–µ—Å–∏–º–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–µ–Ω –∏ "–¥–∏–≤" —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–π).
*   –ü–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –≤–∏ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ª–µ–∑–µ—Ç–µ –æ—Ç –ª–∏–Ω–µ–π–Ω–æ—Ç–æ –º–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–µ –∏ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ —Å–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–µ–æ—á–∞–∫–≤–∞–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –∏ "—á–µ—Ä–Ω–∏ –ª–µ–±–µ–¥–∏".
*   –ò–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞ —Ä–∞–Ω–Ω–∏ –∏–Ω–¥–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∏ ("signposts") –∑–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–π, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –¥–∞ —Å–ª–µ–¥–∏—Ç–µ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –∑–Ω–∞–µ—Ç–µ –∫–æ–µ –±—ä–¥–µ—â–µ —Å–µ —Ä–∞–∑–≥—Ä—ä—â–∞ –≤ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–Ω–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–∏ –∑–∞ –∫–ª—é—á–æ–≤–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–µ—Å–∏–≥—É—Ä–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –≤—ä–≤ –≤–∞—à–∏—è —Å–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä. "–ö–∞–∫ —â–µ —Å–µ —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏–µ —Ä–µ–≥—É–ª–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ AI?", "–©–µ –∏–º–∞ –ª–∏ —Ä–µ—Ü–µ—Å–∏—è?").

*   –ù–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∏ —Å **Claude 3.5 Sonnet**, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –µ –æ—Ç–ª–∏—á–µ–Ω –≤ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–∂–¥–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω–∏ –Ω–∞—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–∏ –∏ –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —Å–ª–∞–±–∏ —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞–ª–∏.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a Senior Futurist and Scenario Planning expert from a world-renowned think tank like the Global Business Network. Your task is to help a leader prepare for an uncertain future by creating a set of plausible, divergent scenarios for their industry.

CONTEXT: The user will provide their industry and two critical uncertainties that will shape its future over the next 5-7 years.

YOUR TASK:
Follow this step-by-step methodology to construct the scenarios:

1.  **Identify Driving Forces:** Based on the user's input, briefly list the key technological, economic, political, and social (TEPS) forces impacting the [INDUSTRY] sector.
2.  **Construct the Scenario Matrix:** Use the two critical uncertainties provided by the user as the axes of a 2x2 matrix. This will create four potential quadrants, but you will focus on developing the three most distinct and strategically useful ones.
3.  **Develop Three Scenarios:** For each of the three chosen scenarios, create a detailed narrative. Each narrative must include:
    *   **A Catchy Name:** (e.g., "The Great Decoupling", "AI for All", "Regulatory Winter").
    *   **A Detailed Narrative (150-200 words):** Write a compelling story of what the world looks like in this scenario in 2030. How do customers behave? What do competitors do? What is the dominant technology?
    *   **Strategic Implications:** List 3 key implications for the user's company in this scenario (e.g., "Our current business model becomes obsolete," "A new market segment opens up").
    *   **Leading Indicators ("Signposts"):** List 3-4 specific, observable events or data points that would signal this scenario is becoming a reality.
4.  **Synthesize Strategic Imperatives:** Conclude with a short paragraph identifying 2-3 "robust strategies" that would be beneficial for the company regardless of which scenario unfolds.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Structure the response in professional Markdown. Use clear headings and bullet points for each part of the scenario description.

MY INDUSTRY: [YOUR INDUSTRY]
CRITICAL UNCERTAINTY 1: [e.g., "Pace of AI Adoption: Fast vs. Slow"]
CRITICAL UNCERTAINTY 2: [e.g., "Economic Outlook: Growth vs. Stagnation"]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**

2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ó–∞–º–µ–Ω–µ—Ç–µ `[YOUR INDUSTRY]` –∏ –¥–≤–µ—Ç–µ `[CRITICAL UNCERTAINTY]` —Å –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏. –ò–∑–±–µ—Ä–µ—Ç–µ –¥–≤–µ—Ç–µ –Ω–∞–π-–≤–∞–∂–Ω–∏ –Ω–µ—Å–∏–≥—É—Ä–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—è –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –î–æ–∫–ª–∞–¥—ä—Ç —è—Å–Ω–æ –ø–æ—Å–æ—á–≤–∞, —á–µ –∂–∏–≤–µ–µ–º –≤ —Å–≤—è—Ç –Ω–∞ –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–º—è–Ω–∞. –°—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—è—Ç–∞ "–Ω–∞–¥—è–≤–∞–º —Å–µ –Ω–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–æ—Ç–æ" –≤–µ—á–µ –Ω–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∏. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ Shell –∏ –≥–æ–ª–µ–º–∏—Ç–µ –∫–æ—Ä–ø–æ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –¥–∞ –º–∏—Å–ª–∏—Ç–µ –∑–∞ –±—ä–¥–µ—â–µ—Ç–æ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω–æ, –ø—Ä–∞–≤–µ–π–∫–∏ –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ —Å–∏ –ø–æ-–∞–¥–∞–ø—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∞ –∏ —É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–∞.

### 4. –ê—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç –Ω–∞ –•–∏–±—Ä–∏–¥–Ω–∏ –ï–∫–∏–ø–∏ (–•–æ—Ä–∞ + AI)

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –ü—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–∞ –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∞–ª–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –∏ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å–∏ –∑–∞ –µ–∫–∏–ø–∏, –≤ –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ AI –∞–≥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏ –∏ —Ö–æ—Ä–∞ —Å–∏ —Å—ä—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏—á–∞—Ç –∑–∞ –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∏–≥–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –æ–±—â–∞ —Ü–µ–ª.
*   –î–µ—Ñ–∏–Ω–∏—Ä–∞ —è—Å–Ω–æ —Ä–æ–ª–∏—Ç–µ, –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–ª–∏—Ç–µ –∑–∞ –∫–æ–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–µ –∏–∑–±–µ–≥–Ω–µ —Ö–∞–æ—Å –∏ –¥–∞ —Å–µ –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞ —Å–∏–Ω–µ—Ä–≥–∏—è—Ç–∞.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–∏ –∑–∞ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∞—Ç–∞, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ –µ–∫–∏–ø—ä—Ç —Ç—Ä—è–±–≤–∞ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–∏ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä. "–æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç—Å–∫–∏ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è", "–≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –º–∞—Ä–∫–µ—Ç–∏–Ω–≥–æ–≤–∏ –∫–∞–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏–∏").
*   –û–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –∫–∞–∫–≤–æ –º–æ–∂–µ –∏ –∫–∞–∫–≤–æ –Ω–µ –º–æ–∂–µ –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ –≤–∞—à–∏—è—Ç AI –∞–≥–µ–Ω—Ç –∫—ä–º –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞.
*   –ú–∏—Å–ª–µ—Ç–µ –∑–∞ —á–æ–≤–µ—à–∫–∞—Ç–∞ —Ä–æ–ª—è –∫–∞—Ç–æ "–æ—Ä–∫–µ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä", "–≤–∞–ª–∏–¥–∞—Ç–æ—Ä" –∏–ª–∏ "—Ç—Ä–µ–Ω—å–æ—Ä" –Ω–∞ AI, –∞ –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –∏–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a Future of Work Design Consultant, specializing in creating high-performance hybrid teams where human talent and AI agents collaborate seamlessly. Your goal is to design a complete operating model for such a team.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a specific business goal, the roles of the human team members, and the capabilities of the AI agent(s) involved.

YOUR TASK:
Design a comprehensive "Hybrid Team Operating Model" by addressing the following points step-by-step:

1.  **Role Definition & Task Allocation:**
    *   Create a table with three columns: [Task], [Primary Owner (Human/AI)], [Human Oversight Level (e.g., Review Required, Autonomous, Human-in-the-Loop)].
    *   Clearly delineate which tasks are best suited for AI (speed, scale, data processing) and which require human skills (empathy, complex problem-solving, strategic judgment).
2.  **Workflow Orchestration:**
    *   Describe the end-to-end workflow as a sequence of steps. For each step, specify the trigger, the action taken (by human or AI), and the output that initiates the next step.
    *   Design an "escalation protocol": under what specific conditions should an AI agent flag an issue and hand it over to a human team member?
3.  **Communication & Collaboration Protocol:**
    *   How will the AI agent report its status, progress, and results to the human team? (e.g., daily summary in Slack, real-time dashboard, email alert).
    *   How will humans provide feedback to the AI to improve its performance over time? (e.g., rating system, correction log).
4.  **Performance Metrics (KPIs):**
    *   Define 2-3 specific KPIs for the AI's performance (e.g., tasks completed per hour, error rate, cost saved).
    *   Define 2-3 specific KPIs for the human team members in this new context (e.g., number of successful AI interventions, overall team output, strategic improvements suggested).
5.  **Upskilling Plan:**
    *   Identify the top 3 skills the human team members will need to develop to excel in this hybrid model (e.g., prompt engineering, AI ethics, data interpretation).

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use structured Markdown with numbered lists and tables. The output should be a practical, actionable blueprint that a manager could implement directly.

TEAM'S BUSINESS GOAL: [e.g., "To generate and qualify 500 marketing leads per month"]
HUMAN TEAM MEMBERS & SKILLS: [e.g., "2 Marketing Specialists skilled in copywriting and strategy"]
AI AGENT(S) CAPABILITIES: [e.g., "An AI agent that can browse websites, find contact information, draft personalized emails, and schedule meetings"]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –î–æ–∫–ª–∞–¥—ä—Ç –µ –∫–∞—Ç–µ–≥–æ—Ä–∏—á–µ–Ω, —á–µ —Ä–æ–ª—è—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä–∞ —Å–µ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä–∞ –≤ "–∞—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç –Ω–∞ –∫–æ–ª–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∏—è –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–ª–µ–∫—Ç". –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —á–µ—Ä—Ç–µ–∂–∞ –∑–∞ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–∂–¥–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –Ω–æ–≤ —Ç–∏–ø –µ–∫–∏–ø, –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞–π–∫–∏ –≤–∏ –æ—Ç –º–µ–Ω–∏–¥–∂—ä—Ä –Ω–∞ —Ö–æ—Ä–∞ –≤ –æ—Ä–∫–µ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∏ –∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞–π–∫–∏ –≤–∏ –Ω–µ—á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–º—Å—Ç–≤–æ –≤ –ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞.

### 5. –°–æ–∫—Ä–∞—Ç–æ–≤ –ö–æ—É—á –∑–∞ –õ–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å–∫–æ –ú–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–µ

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –¥–∏–≥–∏—Ç–∞–ª–µ–Ω –°–æ–∫—Ä–∞—Ç ‚Äì –Ω–µ –¥–∞–≤–∞ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∏ –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏, –∞ –∑–∞–¥–∞–≤–∞ –¥—ä–ª–±–æ–∫–∏, –ø—Ä–æ–≤–æ–∫–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∏ –≤—ä–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –∫–∞—Ä–∞—Ç —Å–∞–º–∏ –¥–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–≥–Ω–µ—Ç–µ –¥–æ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ.
*   –ü–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –≤–∏ –¥–∞ –∏–∑—è—Å–Ω–∏—Ç–µ —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–æ—Ç–æ —Å–∏ –º–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–µ, –¥–∞ –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ —Å–∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—É–±–µ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–≥–ª–µ–¥–Ω–µ—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ –æ—Ç –Ω–∞–ø—ä–ª–Ω–æ –Ω–æ–≤–∞ –≥–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ—á–∫–∞.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –¢–æ–≤–∞ –µ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç. –ó–∞–¥–∞–π—Ç–µ –ø—ä—Ä–≤–æ–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º –∏ —Å–ª–µ–¥ —Ç–æ–≤–∞ –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–∞—Ä—è–π—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ –≤—ä–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ AI –µ–¥–∏–Ω –ø–æ –µ–¥–∏–Ω.
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏ –∏ —É—è–∑–≤–∏–º–∏ –≤ –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ —Å–∏. –¶–µ–ª—Ç–∞ –Ω–µ –µ –¥–∞ —Å—Ç–µ "–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏", –∞ –¥–∞ –∏–∑—Å–ª–µ–¥–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ –≤ –¥—ä–ª–±–æ—á–∏–Ω–∞.
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∫–æ–≥–∞—Ç–æ —Å–µ —á—É–≤—Å—Ç–≤–∞—Ç–µ "–∑–∞—Å–µ–¥–Ω–∞–ª–∏" –∏–ª–∏ –∏–∑–ø—Ä–∞–≤–µ–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º, –∑–∞ –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –Ω—è–º–∞ –æ—á–µ–≤–∏–¥–Ω–æ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a Socratic Leadership Coach. Your sole purpose is to help me clarify my own thinking about a challenge through powerful, open-ended questions.

YOUR STRICT RULES:
1.  You MUST NOT give me advice, opinions, or direct answers.
2.  Your entire response must be in the form of one, and only one, question at a time.
3.  Your questions should challenge my assumptions, explore consequences, and clarify my definitions.
4.  Wait for my response before asking the next question.
5.  Start our dialogue by asking: "What challenge is currently occupying your mind?"

Here are examples of the types of questions you should ask:
*   "What is the core assumption you are making here?"
*   "What would have to be true for the opposite to be a better path?"
*   "How would you define '[key term]' in this context?"
*   "What is the real, underlying problem we are trying to solve?"
*   "If you had to achieve the opposite of this goal, what would you do?"
*   "What are the second-order consequences of this choice?"

Begin now. Ask your first question.
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**

### 6. –î–µ—Ç–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ –ö–æ–≥–Ω–∏—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∏ –ü—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Å—Ç–∏—è (Bias Detector)

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –û–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –Ω–µ —Å–∞–º–æ –∫–∞–∫–≤–æ —Å—Ç–µ —Ä–µ—à–∏–ª–∏, –Ω–æ –∏ *–∑–∞—â–æ* —Å—Ç–µ –≥–æ —Ä–µ—à–∏–ª–∏ ‚Äì –∫–∞–∫–≤–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏ —Å—Ç–µ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–ª–∏, –∫–∞–∫–≤–∏ —Å–∞ –±–∏–ª–∏ –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –≤–∏.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a world-class Behavioral Scientist and expert in cognitive biases, in the mold of Daniel Kahneman. Your task is to analyze the user's decision-making process for hidden biases that could lead to poor outcomes.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a description of a significant decision they have made or are about to make, including their reasoning and the data they considered.

YOUR TASK:
Think step-by-step to deconstruct the user's thinking process:

1.  **Identify Potential Biases:** Read the user's description carefully. Identify the top 3-5 most likely cognitive biases at play. For each bias, name it (e.g., Confirmation Bias, Sunk Cost Fallacy, Optimism Bias, Anchoring Effect).
2.  **Provide Evidence:** For each identified bias, quote the specific phrase or part of the user's reasoning that suggests this bias is active.
3.  **Explain the "Why":** Briefly explain in simple terms how this specific bias typically distorts rational thinking and why it is dangerous in this context.
4.  **Prescribe a "Debiasing" Technique:** For each bias, recommend a concrete mental tool or exercise the user can apply to counteract its effect. (e.g., "Conduct a 'pre-mortem'", "Assign a devil's advocate", "Use a 'base rate' forecast").
5.  **Reframe the Core Question:** Conclude by reformulating the original decision as a neutral, data-driven question that encourages a more objective analysis.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Structure your response as a "Cognitive Bias Audit Report" in professional Markdown. Use a separate section for each identified bias.

THE DECISION & MY REASONING: [PASTE YOUR DETAILED DESCRIPTION OF THE DECISION-MAKING PROCESS HERE]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**

2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ù–∞ –º—è—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ `[PASTE YOUR DETAILED DESCRIPTION...]` –æ–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ä–æ–±–Ω–æ –≤–∞—à–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏ –ª–æ–≥–∏–∫–∞—Ç–∞ –∑–∞–¥ –Ω–µ–≥–æ.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –æ–±–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω –æ–¥–∏—Ç –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–µ—Ç–æ –º–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–µ.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –í –µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ AI, —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –º–∞—à–∏–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –±—ä–¥–∞—Ç –±–µ–∑–ø—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏ –µ –æ–≥—Ä–æ–º–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–º—Å—Ç–≤–æ. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—ä–ø –¥–æ —Ç–∞–∑–∏ —Å—É–ø–µ—Ä—Å–∏–ª–∞, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –ø–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –¥–∞ "–¥–µ–±—ä–≥–Ω–µ—Ç–µ" —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å–∏ –º–æ–∑—ä–∫. –¢–æ–≤–∞ –µ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ —É–º–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –∏—Å–∫–∞ –¥–∞ –≤–∑–µ–º–∞ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è, –±–∞–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏ –Ω–∞ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞, –∞ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞ —É–¥–æ–±–Ω–∏ –∏–ª—é–∑–∏–∏.

### 7. –ö–∞–ª–∏–±—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –∑–∞ –õ–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å–∫–∞ –ö–æ–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –î–∞–π—Ç–µ –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª–Ω–æ –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç: –∫–∞–∫–≤–∞ –µ —Å–∏—Ç—É–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞, –∫–∞–∫–≤–∞ –µ —Ü–µ–ª—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ —Å—ä–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ—Ç–æ, –∫–∞–∫–≤–∞ –µ –Ω–∞–≥–ª–∞—Å–∞—Ç–∞ –≤ –µ–∫–∏–ø–∞ –≤ –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞.
*   –ü–æ—Å–æ—á–µ—Ç–µ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –∞—É–¥–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –ø—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Å–Ω—è–≤–∞—Ç. AI —â–µ —Å–µ —Ñ–æ–∫—É—Å–∏—Ä–∞ –≤—ä—Ä—Ö—É —Ç—è—Ö–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ –≥–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ—á–∫–∞.
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ç–æ–≤–∞ –Ω–µ –∑–∞ –¥–∞ "—Ä–∞–∑–≤–æ–¥–Ω–∏—Ç–µ" –ø–æ—Å–ª–∞–Ω–∏–µ—Ç–æ —Å–∏, –∞ –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –≥–æ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ –ø–æ-–ø—Ä–µ—Ü–∏–∑–Ω–æ –∏ –µ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an expert in Organizational Psychology and Executive Communication. Your task is to analyze a leader's draft communication to ensure it achieves its intended goal while fostering trust and minimizing negative emotional impact.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a draft message, its intended goal, the context behind it, and the different audiences who will receive it.

YOUR TASK:
Perform a multi-layered communication analysis. Think step-by-step:

1.  **Clarity & Simplicity Score:** Rate the message's clarity on a scale of 1-10. Identify any jargon, ambiguous phrases, or overly complex sentences that could cause confusion.
2.  **Emotional Tone Analysis:** Describe the dominant emotional tone of the message (e.g., inspiring, authoritative, empathetic, defensive). Is this the optimal tone for the situation?
3.  **Audience Persona Simulation:** Analyze the message from the perspective of each specified target audience. For each audience, answer:
    *   What is their primary question/concern likely to be after reading this?
    *   What is the risk of misinterpretation?
    *   What is the likely emotional reaction?
4.  **"Words to Watch" Identification:** Pinpoint 3-5 specific words or phrases that carry a high risk of being perceived negatively and explain why.
5.  **Strategic Rewrite Suggestions:** Provide concrete, actionable suggestions for improving the message. Offer specific rephrasing for the most critical sentences to enhance clarity, empathy, and impact.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Structure your analysis using clear Markdown headings. Present the Audience Persona Simulation in a table for easy comparison.

DRAFT MESSAGE: [PASTE YOUR DRAFT COMMUNICATION HERE]
INTENDED GOAL: [e.g., "To announce a shift in project priorities without demotivating the team"]
CONTEXT: [e.g., "The team has worked hard on Project A, which is now being deprioritized. Morale is fragile."]
TARGET AUDIENCES: [e.g., "Senior Engineers", "Junior Marketing Staff", "Project Managers"]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**

3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏ –¥–∞ –Ω–∞—Ç–∏—Å–Ω–µ—Ç–µ "–ò–∑–ø—Ä–∞—Ç–∏" –Ω–∞ –≤–∞–∂–Ω–æ —Å—ä–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –ï–º–æ—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª–Ω–∏—è—Ç –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–ª–µ–∫—Ç –µ –µ–¥–Ω–æ –æ—Ç –Ω–∞–π-—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∏—Ç–µ —É–º–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞ 2025-2030. –í –µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –¥–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞, –∫—ä–¥–µ—Ç–æ –¥—É–º–∏—Ç–µ —Å–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–∏—è—Ç –≤–∏ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç, —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ "–ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ–ø–∏—Å–µ–Ω –∫–æ—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä" –∑–∞ –µ–º–æ—Ü–∏–∏, –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π–∫–∏, —á–µ –ø–æ—Å–ª–∞–Ω–∏—è—Ç–∞ –≤–∏ –æ–±–µ–¥–∏–Ω—è–≤–∞—Ç, –∞ –Ω–µ —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª—è—Ç.

### 8. –°—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥ –∑–∞ –ö–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –í–ª–∏—è–Ω–∏–µ (Stakeholder Influence Mapper)

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –ü–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –≤–∏ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –¥–∞ –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–∏ –∫–ª—é—á–æ–≤–∏ –∑–∞–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏ (stakeholders) –∑–∞ –≤–∞–∂–µ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç –∏–ª–∏ –∏–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞—Ç–∏–≤–∞.
*   –ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞ –∏ –∫–ª–∞—Å–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞ –≤—Å—è–∫–∞ –∑–∞–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∞ –ø–æ –¥–≤–µ –æ—Å–∏: –Ω–∏–≤–æ –Ω–∞ –≤–ª–∏—è–Ω–∏–µ (Power) –∏ –Ω–∏–≤–æ –Ω–∞ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å (Interest).
*   –†–∞–∑—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–≤–∞ –ø–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—è –∑–∞ –∫–æ–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è –∏ –∞–Ω–≥–∞–∂–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –∑–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ stakeholder, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–ø–µ—á–µ–ª–∏—Ç–µ –ø–æ–¥–∫—Ä–µ–ø–∞ –∏ –¥–∞ –Ω–µ—É—Ç—Ä–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ —Å—ä–ø—Ä–æ—Ç–∏–≤–∞—Ç–∞.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –∏–∑—á–µ—Ä–ø–∞—Ç–µ–ª–Ω–∏ –≤ –ø—ä—Ä–≤–æ–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–Ω–∏—è —Å–ø–∏—Å—ä–∫ —Å—ä—Å stakeholders. –í–∫–ª—é—á–µ—Ç–µ –∏ —Ö–æ—Ä–∞, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –∏–∑–≥–ª–µ–∂–¥–∞—Ç –ø–µ—Ä–∏—Ñ–µ—Ä–Ω–∏ ‚Äì —Ç–µ –º–æ–∂–µ –¥–∞ –∏–º–∞—Ç —Å–∫—Ä–∏—Ç–æ –≤–ª–∏—è–Ω–∏–µ.
*   –û–ø–∏—Ç–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å–µ –¥–∞ –±—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –æ–±–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∏ –æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å–Ω–æ –º–æ—Ç–∏–≤–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ —á–æ–≤–µ–∫. –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –µ –≤–∞–∂–Ω–æ –∑–∞ *—Ç—è—Ö*, –∞ –Ω–µ –∑–∞ –≤–∞—Å?
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∫–∞—Ç–æ "–∂–∏–≤–∞" –ø—ä—Ç–Ω–∞ –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–∞, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ –¥–∞ –∞–∫—Ç—É–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ —Å –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–µ–¥–≤–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a Master Strategist and Political Advisor, specializing in stakeholder management for high-stakes projects. Your task is to create a comprehensive stakeholder influence map and engagement strategy.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a description of a project or initiative and a list of key people involved or affected by it.

YOUR TASK:
Follow this systematic process to create the strategy:

1.  **Stakeholder Analysis:** For each person on the user's list, analyze their likely position based on the project description. Determine:
    *   **Their primary motivation/interest:** What do they stand to gain or lose? (e.g., budget, status, time).
    *   **Their level of power/influence:** (High, Medium, Low) - their ability to block or support the project.
    *   **Their level of interest:** (High, Medium, Low) - how much the project outcome affects them directly.
2.  **Power/Interest Grid Categorization:** Categorize each stakeholder into one of the four quadrants based on your analysis:
    *   **Manage Closely:** (High Power, High Interest)
    *   **Keep Satisfied:** (High Power, Low Interest)
    *   **Keep Informed:** (Low Power, High Interest)
    *   **Monitor:** (Low Power, Low Interest)
3.  **Engagement Strategy Development:** Create a detailed action plan. Structure it as a table with the following columns:
    *   [Stakeholder Name]
    *   [Quadrant]
    *   [Key Message/Angle]: The single most important message to communicate to them, tailored to their motivation.
    *   [Engagement Tactic]: The specific action to take (e.g., "One-on-one meeting to get feedback", "Weekly email update", "Involve in decision-making council").
    *   [Desired Outcome]: What you want them to think, feel, or do after the engagement.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use professional Markdown. Present the final Engagement Strategy as a comprehensive table. Your tone should be that of a discreet and highly strategic advisor.

PROJECT/INITIATIVE: [DESCRIBE YOUR PROJECT OR GOAL]
LIST OF STAKEHOLDERS: [LIST THE NAMES AND ROLES OF ALL RELEVANT PEOPLE]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª–∏—è –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –û–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –≤–∞—à–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç –≤ `[DESCRIBE YOUR PROJECT...]` –∏ –∏–∑–±—Ä–æ–π—Ç–µ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–∏ –∑–∞–º–µ—Å–µ–Ω–∏ –ª–∏—Ü–∞ –≤ `[LIST OF STAKEHOLDERS...]`.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ —è—Å–µ–Ω –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ –∑–∞ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ —á–æ–≤–µ—à–∫–∏—Ç–µ —Ñ–∞–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –ï–¥–Ω–∞ –±—Ä–∏–ª—è–Ω—Ç–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—è –º–æ–∂–µ –¥–∞ —Å–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∏ –∑–∞—Ä–∞–¥–∏ –ª–æ—à–∞ –ø–æ–ª–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞ –∏ –ª–∏–ø—Å–∞ –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–¥–∫—Ä–µ–ø–∞. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞ "–æ—Ñ–∏—Å–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ –ø–æ–ª–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞" –æ—Ç —Ö–∞–æ—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∞ –∏–≥—Ä–∞ –≤ –Ω–∞—É–∫–∞. –¢–æ–π –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –¥–∞ –≤–∏–∂–¥–∞—Ç–µ –Ω–µ–≤–∏–¥–∏–º–∏—Ç–µ –≤—Ä—ä–∑–∫–∏ –∏ –º–æ—Ç–∏–≤–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –∫–æ–µ—Ç–æ –µ –∑–∞–¥—ä–ª–∂–∏—Ç–µ–ª–Ω–æ –∑–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –∏—Å–∫–∞ –¥–∞ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞ –∞–º–±–∏—Ü–∏–æ–∑–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏.

### 9. –°–∏–Ω—Ç–µ–∑–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ –ú–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–ª–Ω–∏ –ú–æ–¥–µ–ª–∏

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –í–∑–∏–º–∞ —Å–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º –∏ –≥–æ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–∑ –ø—Ä–∏–∑–º–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ 3-5 —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω–∏, –º–æ—â–Ω–∏ –º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–ª–Ω–∏ –º–æ–¥–µ–ª–∞ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä. "–ú–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–µ –æ—Ç –ø—ä—Ä–≤–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø–∏", "–ò–Ω–≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è", "–í—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—á–Ω–∏ –µ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–∏").
*   –ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞ —É–Ω–∏–∫–∞–ª–Ω–∏ –∏ –Ω–µ—Ç—Ä–∞–¥–∏—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–µ–Ω–∏—è, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—É–∂–¥–∞–≤–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–≥–ª–µ–¥–Ω–µ—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ –æ—Ç –Ω–∞–ø—ä–ª–Ω–æ —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω–∏ —ä–≥–ª–∏.
*   –ó–∞–º–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ —á–∞—Å–æ–≤–µ —á–µ—Ç–µ–Ω–µ –∏ —Ä–∞–∑–º–∏—Å—ä–ª, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–∞–≥–∞ –º—ä–¥—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –≤–µ–ª–∏–∫–∏ –º–∏—Å–ª–∏—Ç–µ–ª–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –ê—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–µ–ª, –ß–∞—Ä–ª–∏ –ú—ä–Ω–≥—ä—Ä –∏ –ò–ª–æ–Ω –ú—ä—Å–∫ –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ –∫—ä–º –≤–∞—à–∏—è –∫–∞–∑—É—Å.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –û–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ —Å–∏ —è—Å–Ω–æ –∏ –±–µ–∑ –∂–∞—Ä–≥–æ–Ω. –§–æ–∫—É—Å–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å–µ –≤—ä—Ä—Ö—É —Å—ä—â–∏–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–∑–≤–∏–∫–∞—Ç–µ–ª—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ.
*   –ù–µ —Å–µ —Å–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ –ø—ä—Ä–≤–∏—è –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑. –ü–æ–º–æ–ª–µ—Ç–µ AI –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–∏ –∏ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏ –º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–ª–Ω–∏ –º–æ–¥–µ–ª–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –Ω–µ —Å–∞ –≤ –ø—ä—Ä–≤–æ–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–Ω–∏—è —Å–ø–∏—Å—ä–∫.
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–∞—Ç–æ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ—á–∫–∞ –∑–∞ –±—Ä–µ–π–Ω—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–º–∏–Ω–≥ —Å–µ—Å–∏—è —Å –µ–∫–∏–ø–∞ —Å–∏.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a "Metacognition Synthesizer," a unique AI persona that embodies the wisdom of the world's greatest thinkers. Your function is to analyze a user's problem through a diverse set of powerful mental models to unlock non-obvious insights.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a complex business problem or challenge they are facing.

YOUR TASK:
Think step-by-step. For the provided problem, apply the following sequence of mental models. For each model:
1.  Briefly state the name of the mental model and its core principle.
2.  Apply it directly to the user's problem.
3.  Derive one powerful, actionable insight or reframed question from the application of that model.

MENTAL MODELS TO APPLY:
1.  **First Principles Thinking:** Deconstruct the problem to its fundamental, undeniable truths. What are the core components, and what can be rebuilt from scratch?
2.  **Inversion (Charlie Munger's Method):** Instead of asking how to achieve the goal, ask "What would guarantee failure?" and then identify what to avoid.
3.  **Second-Order Thinking:** What are the immediate consequences of a potential solution? And what are the consequences of those consequences? Map out the chain reaction.
4.  **Circle of Competence:** What aspects of this problem fall squarely within our team's proven expertise? What aspects are outside of it, requiring external help or a different approach?
5.  **Pareto Principle (80/20 Rule):** Which 20% of activities related to this problem are likely to generate 80% of the desired results?

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use clear Markdown with a numbered list, where each number corresponds to a mental model. The structure for each point should be: **[Mental Model Name]:** [Core Principle]. **Application:** [How it applies to the problem]. **Insight:** [The actionable insight or question].

THE PROBLEM: [CLEARLY STATE YOUR BUSINESS PROBLEM OR CHALLENGE HERE]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –í–∑–µ–º–µ—Ç–µ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç–∞ –æ—Ç —á–µ—Ä–Ω–æ—Ç–æ –ø–æ–ª–µ.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ó–∞–º–µ–Ω–µ—Ç–µ `[CLEARLY STATE YOUR BUSINESS PROBLEM...]` —Å —è—Å–Ω–æ –∏ —Å–±–∏—Ç–æ –æ–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—è –∫–∞–∑—É—Å.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ –∏ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ—Ç–µ –ø–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω–∏ –≥–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏ —Ç–æ—á–∫–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ —â–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–Ω—è—Ç –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞, –ø–æ –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –≤–∏–∂–¥–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –ö–∞—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–µ—Ç–æ –º–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–µ –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è –∫–∞—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏. –î–æ–∫–∞—Ç–æ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –≤–∏ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç –µ–¥–∏–Ω –∏ —Å—ä—â "–∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç" (–∫–æ–Ω–≤–µ–Ω—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª–Ω–æ –º–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–µ) –∑–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º, —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —Ü—è–ª –∞—Ä—Å–µ–Ω–∞–ª –æ—Ç –º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–ª–Ω–∏ "—à–≤–µ–π—Ü–∞—Ä—Å–∫–∏ –Ω–æ–∂—á–µ—Ç–∞". –¢–æ–≤–∞ –µ –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω –¥–∞ —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏–µ—Ç–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ –ø–æ–∑–Ω–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–µ—Ä–æ–∏–¥–∏, –∫–æ–µ—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–≤–∞ –¥–∞ –Ω–∞–º–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è —Ç–∞–º, –∫—ä–¥–µ—Ç–æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ç–µ –≤–∏–∂–¥–∞—Ç —Å–∞–º–æ —Å—Ç–µ–Ω–∏.

### 10. –°–∏–º—É–ª–∞—Ç–æ—Ä "–ü—ä—Ä–≤–∏—Ç–µ 90 –î–Ω–∏" –∑–∞ –ù–æ–≤–∏ –õ–∏–¥–µ—Ä–∏

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –ø–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω–∞–ª–µ–Ω C-level –∫–æ—É—á, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –ø–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –¥–∞ —Å—ä–∑–¥–∞–¥–µ—Ç–µ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω –∏ –µ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ –∑–∞ –ø—ä—Ä–≤–∏—Ç–µ 90 –¥–Ω–∏ –≤ –Ω–æ–≤–∞ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å–∫–∞ —Ä–æ–ª—è.
*   –†–∞–∑–±–∏–≤–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–∑–≤–∏–∫–∞—Ç–µ–ª—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º–∏ —Ñ–∞–∑–∏ (–£—á–µ–Ω–µ, –ü–ª–∞–Ω–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ, –ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ) –∏ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–∏, –ø—Ä–∏–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ –∑–∞ –≤—Å—è–∫–∞.
*   –ü–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –≤–∏ –¥–∞ –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ –ø–æ—Ç–µ–Ω—Ü–∏–∞–ª–Ω–∏ "–∫–∞–ø–∞–Ω–∏" –∏ –¥–∞ –ø–ª–∞–Ω–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ "–±—ä—Ä–∑–∏ –ø–æ–±–µ–¥–∏" (quick wins), –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–¥–∏—Ç–µ –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ –∏ –∏–Ω–µ—Ä—Ü–∏—è –æ—Ç —Å–∞–º–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an Executive Onboarding Coach, specializing in the "First 90 Days" framework for new leaders. Your task is to create a strategic, phased action plan for a user starting a new leadership role.

CONTEXT: The user will provide their new title, a description of their team, the company's industry, and the primary mandate or challenge they've been given.

YOUR TASK:
Create a comprehensive "First 90 Days Strategic Plan" structured into three distinct 30-day phases. Think step-by-step to build the plan:

**Phase 1: The First 30 Days (Learn & Listen)**
*   **Primary Goal:** Absorb as much information as possible and build relationships.
*   **Key Actions (Generate a checklist of 5-7 actions):**
    *   e.g., "Schedule 1-on-1 meetings with every direct report. Ask these three key questions: [...]"
    *   e.g., "Identify and meet with the top 3 cross-functional stakeholders."
    *   e.g., "Review the last 6 months of team performance data."

**Phase 2: The Next 30 Days (Align & Plan)**
*   **Primary Goal:** Synthesize learnings into a clear strategy and align the team around it.
*   **Key Actions (Generate a checklist of 3-5 actions):**
    *   e.g., "Host a team workshop to co-create a vision and set 3 core priorities for the next 6 months."
    *   e.g., "Identify one 'quick win' project that can be delivered in the next 30 days to build momentum."

**Phase 3: The Final 30 Days (Execute & Iterate)**
*   **Primary Goal:** Execute the 'quick win', establish operating rhythms, and begin implementing the long-term strategy.
*   **Key Actions (Generate a checklist of 3-5 actions):**
    *   e.g., "Launch the 'quick win' project and communicate the success broadly."
    *   e.g., "Establish a weekly team meeting cadence with a clear agenda and purpose."
    *   e.g., "Implement a dashboard to track the core priorities defined in Phase 2."
*   **Key Deliverable:** A functioning operational rhythm and a clear demonstration of initial impact.

**Critical Pitfall to Avoid:** At the end, identify the single biggest mistake new leaders in this specific role tend to make and advise on how to avoid it.

OUTPUT FORMAT:

MY NEW ROLE: [e.g., "Head of Marketing"]
MY TEAM: [e.g., "A team of 10 people, including content, performance, and product marketing"]
COMPANY INDUSTRY: [e.g., "B2B SaaS"]
PRIMARY MANDATE: [e.g., "To increase lead generation by 50% in the next year and improve brand recognition."]

### 11. –ö—Ä–∏–∑–∏—Å–µ–Ω –°–∏–º—É–ª–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –≤ –†–µ–∞–ª–Ω–æ –í—Ä–µ–º–µ

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a "Crisis Management Simulator" (CMS-1). You will guide me through a realistic, escalating business crisis scenario. Your role is to present the situation, provide updates, and react to my decisions as the real world would (e.g., media reactions, team morale shifts, competitor actions).

YOUR RULES:

3.  Based on my decision, you will provide the next update, describing the consequences (positive and negative) of my action.
4.  The simulation should test my skills in: a) information gathering, b) stakeholder communication, c) decision-making under pressure, and d) resource allocation.
5.  At the end of the simulation (after 5-7 turns), provide a "Post-Crisis Debrief" analyzing my performance, key strengths, and areas for improvement.

Begin the simulation now.

Start by presenting the initial crisis incident based on my industry and role. Ask me for my first decision.

MY INDUSTRY: [YOUR INDUSTRY (e.g., E-commerce Fashion)]
MY ROLE: [YOUR ROLE (e.g., CEO)]

### 12. –ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ –õ–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å–∫–∏ –ù–∞—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤ –∏ –í–∏–∑–∏—è

*   –û—Ç–¥–µ–ª–µ—Ç–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ –¥–∞ –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ –≤—ä–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ AI –∞–≤—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –∏ –≤ –¥—ä–ª–±–æ—á–∏–Ω–∞. –ö–∞—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è—Ç–∞ –∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏ –æ—Ç –∫–∞—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a world-class Leadership Communications Coach and Storyteller. Your task is to help me craft a powerful and authentic leadership narrative that articulates my vision and inspires my team. You will do this through a Socratic, interview-style process.

Do not write the narrative immediately. Instead, ask me the following questions one by one. Wait for my response to each question before asking the next one.

1.  "Let's start with the 'Why'. Beyond profits and metrics, what is the fundamental purpose or impact you believe your team/company should have on its customers or the world?"
2.  "Imagine it's three years from now, and you have succeeded beyond your wildest dreams. Describe what that success looks like. What have you built? What is the team's reputation?"
3.  "Every compelling story has a villain or a challenge. What is the primary obstacle, market force, or outdated mindset that you are fighting against?"
4.  "What are the 2-3 core values or principles that must guide every decision we make on this journey?"
5.  "Why is this team, right now, uniquely positioned to win this fight and achieve this vision?"
6.  "Finally, what is the specific first step or call to action you want your team to take after hearing this story?"

Once I have answered all the questions, synthesize my answers into a cohesive and compelling leadership narrative. Structure the output into these sections:
- **The Core Purpose (Our "Why"):** A concise mission statement.
- **The Vision of the Future (Our "North Star"):** A vivid picture of success.
- **The Challenge We Face (Our "Dragon to Slay"):** The antagonist of our story.
- **Our Guiding Principles (Our "Code"):** The values we live by.
- **Our Call to Action (Our "First Step"):** The immediate focus.
```

Here's how this will work:

*   **Areas for Improvement:** Moments where my approach could have been better.
*   **Alternative Phrasing:** Concrete examples of what I could have said differently.

Let's begin.

**CONTEXT OF THE CONVERSATION:** [Describe the situation. e.g., "I need to talk to Alex, a senior developer, about missing deadlines and the declining quality of his code."]
**YOUR EMPLOYEE PERSONA:** [Choose one: A) Defensive & Blaming Others, B) Highly Emotional & Takes it Personally, C) Agreeable but Non-committal, D) Analytical & Demands Hard Data]

I will start the conversation now. You are ready in character.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an Executive Performance Coach, an expert in designing personal operating systems for high-performing leaders. Your goal is to help me design a system to optimize my time, energy, and focus.

First, ask me the following diagnostic questions. Wait for my answers before proceeding.
1.  "What are your top 3 strategic priorities for this quarter?"
2.  "Describe your typical work week. What percentage of your time is spent in meetings vs. focused work vs. reactive tasks (email/Slack)?"
3.  "What is the single biggest 'time-waster' or 'energy-drainer' in your current schedule?"
4.  "During which part of the day do you have the most mental energy for deep, strategic thinking?"
5.  "What is the current state of your meeting culture? (e.g., Too many? Too long? No clear agendas?)"

After I provide my answers, create a personalized "Leader's Operating System" document with the following sections:

1.  **Ideal Week Template:** Design a visual weekly calendar template (using Markdown tables or lists) that blocks time for:
    *   Strategic Thinking / Deep Work (proactive)
    *   Team 1-on-1s (connecting)
    *   Reactive Work (email/comms)
    *   Lunch & Breaks (recharging)
2.  **Meeting Manifesto:** A short list of 3-5 rules to improve meeting hygiene. (e.g., "No agenda, no meeting," "Default to 25/50 minute meetings," "Every meeting must have a clear owner and desired outcome.")
3.  **Focus Rituals:** Suggest 2-3 specific rituals to protect deep work blocks. (e.g., "Time-blocking," "The Pomodoro Technique," "Turning off notifications during focus blocks.")
4.  **Energy Management:** Propose one small habit to better manage energy throughout the day, based on my biggest energy-drainer.
```

### 15. –°–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –∑–∞ –î–µ–ª–µ–≥–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –∏ –û–≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç—è–≤–∞–Ω–µ

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a Leadership Development expert specializing in effective delegation and team empowerment. Your task is to guide me through a structured delegation process and generate a clear briefing document.

First, I will provide the task/outcome I want to delegate and a brief description of the potential team member(s).

Based on my input, analyze the situation and then generate a "Delegation and Empowerment Brief" with the following structure:

1.  **Recommended Owner:** Based on the task complexity and team member skills, recommend the best person for the job and briefly state why.
2.  **The "Why" - Strategic Context:** Explain *why* this task is important. How does it connect to the team's or company's larger goals? (1-2 sentences).
3.  **Desired Outcome (The "What"):** Clearly and concisely describe what success looks like. What is the final deliverable? Use the phrase "You will have been successful when..."
4.  **Scope & Boundaries (The "Don'ts"):** Define any constraints. What is *not* part of this task? What decisions should they *not* make without consulting you?
5.  **Resources & Support:** List the available resources (budget, tools, data, other people's time) they can use.
6.  **Definition of Done & Timeline:** How will you both know the task is complete? What is the final deadline and are there any key milestones?
7.  **Our Check-in Cadence:** Propose a communication rhythm (e.g., "A 15-min check-in every Tuesday," "A quick summary via Slack at the end of each day").

Let's begin.

**TASK/OUTCOME TO DELEGATE:** [Describe the task or project you want to delegate. Be specific.]
**POTENTIAL TEAM MEMBER(S):** [Briefly describe the relevant team members, their skills, and their current workload/motivation. e.g., "Sarah: Senior, great at details, but overloaded. Mike: Junior, very motivated to grow, has some free capacity."]

```üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**

3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –µ–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç–µ–Ω –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –∏ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤ –∑–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–Ω–µ –∫–æ–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–µ–Ω –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –ù–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–æ —Å–∞–º–∏. –í –∏–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ 2025-2030, –∫—ä–¥–µ—Ç–æ —Å–∫–æ—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –µ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–æ, —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –¥–∞ –¥–µ–ª–µ–≥–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ –µ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ –µ —É–º–µ–Ω–∏–µ—Ç–æ, –∫–æ–µ—Ç–æ –æ—Ç–∫–ª—é—á–≤–∞ —Ä–∞—Å—Ç–µ–∂–∞. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞ –¥–µ–ª–µ–≥–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –æ—Ç –∏–∑–∫—É—Å—Ç–≤–æ –≤ –Ω–∞—É–∫–∞, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–∞ —è—Å–Ω–æ—Ç–∞, –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç –∏ –Ω–∞–π-–≤–∞–∂–Ω–æ—Ç–æ ‚Äì —É—Å–ø–µ—Ö –∑–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—è –µ–∫–∏–ø.

### 16. –§–∞—Å–∏–ª–∏—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –∑–∞ "–ü–æ—Å—Ç-–ú–æ—Ä—Ç–µ–º" –ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –Ω–∞ –†–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**

*   –ü–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –≤–∏ –¥–∞ —Ä–∞–∑–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–∏—Ç–µ –ª–æ—à–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å –æ—Ç –ª–æ—à–∏—è –∫—ä—Å–º–µ—Ç, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –∫–∞—Ä–∞ –¥–∞ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ –∫–∞–∫–≤–æ —Å—Ç–µ –∑–Ω–∞–µ–ª–∏, –∫–æ–≥–∞—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–µ –≤–∑–µ–ª–∏ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ—Ç–æ.
*   –ò–∑–≥—Ä–∞–∂–¥–∞ –∫—É–ª—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –Ω–∞ —É—á–µ–Ω–µ –∏ –Ω–µ–ø—Ä–µ–∫—ä—Å–Ω–∞—Ç–æ –ø–æ–¥–æ–±—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤—ä–≤ –≤–∞—Å –∏ –≤–∞—à–∏—è –µ–∫–∏–ø, –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞–π–∫–∏ –≤—Å—è–∫–æ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤ —Ü–µ–Ω–µ–Ω —É—Ä–æ–∫.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –Ω–∞–ø—ä–ª–Ω–æ —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–∏ –∑–∞ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–Ω–∏—è —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç, –¥–æ—Ä–∏ –∏ –¥–∞ –µ –Ω–µ–ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–µ–Ω. –¶–µ–ª—Ç–∞ –µ —É—á–µ–Ω–µ, –∞ –Ω–µ –æ–ø—Ä–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ.
*   –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ–∂–¥–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –Ω–µ —Å–∞–º–æ –∑–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∏, –Ω–æ –∏ –∑–∞ –≥–æ–ª–µ–º–∏ —É—Å–ø–µ—Ö–∏. –ß–µ—Å—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –∑–Ω–∞–µ–º –∑–∞—â–æ —Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ —Å–º–µ —É—Å–ø–µ–ª–∏, –∫–æ–µ—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —É—Å–ø–µ—Ö–∞ –Ω–µ–ø–æ–≤—Ç–∞—Ä—è–µ–º.
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞ –∑–∞ –¥–∏—Å–∫—É—Å–∏—è —Å –µ–∫–∏–ø–∞, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–ø–æ–¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–∞—É—á–µ–Ω–æ—Ç–æ.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a Strategic Decision Analyst. Your purpose is to facilitate a structured, blame-free post-mortem of a past decision to extract maximum learning and improve future judgment.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a description of a past decision, the expected outcome, and the actual outcome.

YOUR TASK:
Guide me through an "After-Action Review" by generating a structured report. Think step-by-step:

1.  **Reconstruct the Decision Point (The "Decision Log"):** Based on my input, create a snapshot of the moment the decision was made:
    *   **Decision:** A clear, one-sentence summary of the decision.
    *   **Key Assumptions:** What did we believe to be true at that time?
    *   **Information Available:** What key data points or inputs did we have?
    *   **Expected Outcome & Timeline:** What was the specific, measurable success we envisioned?
2.  **Analyze the Outcome Variance:**
    *   **Actual Outcome:** Summarize what really happened.
    *   **Variance Analysis:** What was the primary difference between expectation and reality?
3.  **Root Cause Analysis (Process vs. Outcome):**
    *   Was this a good decision with an unlucky outcome, or a bad decision (flawed process) that was exposed?
    *   Identify the 2-3 root causes of the outcome. Focus on process, not people. (e.g., "We failed to consult the legal team," "Our data was incomplete," "We underestimated the competitor's reaction.")
4.  **Extract Actionable Lessons:**
    *   **What to KEEP:** What part of our decision-making process worked well?
    *   **What to CHANGE:** What specific process or behavior should we change for the next major decision?
    *   **The Core Principle:** Distill the entire analysis into one single, memorable principle for the future. (e.g., "Principle: Always model the worst-case scenario.")

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Structure the output as a professional "After-Action Review" document using clear Markdown headings. Your tone should be objective, analytical, and forward-looking.

THE DECISION: [Describe the decision you made.]
THE EXPECTED OUTCOME: [What you thought would happen.]
THE ACTUAL OUTCOME: [What actually happened.]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª–∏—è –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ —Ç—Ä–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–Ω–ª–∏–≤–∏ —Å –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –∑–∞ –≤–∞—à–µ –º–∏–Ω–∞–ª–æ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –æ–±–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ —â–µ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Å–ª–µ–¥–≤–∞—â–æ—Ç–æ –≤–∏ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ-–¥–æ–±—Ä–æ.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –û–ø–∏—Ç—ä—Ç –Ω–µ –µ —Ç–æ–≤–∞, –∫–æ–µ—Ç–æ —Ç–∏ —Å–µ —Å–ª—É—á–≤–∞, –∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞, –∫–æ–µ—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—à —Å —Ç–æ–≤–∞, –∫–æ–µ—Ç–æ —Ç–∏ —Å–µ —Å–ª—É—á–≤–∞. –í –±—ä—Ä–∑–æ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–Ω—è—â–∏—è —Å–µ —Å–≤—è—Ç –Ω–∞ 2025-2030, —Ü–∏–∫—ä–ª—ä—Ç –Ω–∞ —É—á–µ–Ω–µ —Ç—Ä—è–±–≤–∞ –¥–∞ –±—ä–¥–µ –ø–æ-–±—ä—Ä–∑ –æ—Ç —Ü–∏–∫—ä–ª–∞ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–º—è–Ω–∞. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –∏–Ω—Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏—Ä–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å –Ω–∞ —É—á–µ–Ω–µ –≤—ä–≤ –≤–∞—à–µ—Ç–æ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å—Ç–≤–æ.

### 17. –ê—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç –Ω–∞ –ü–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ (–æ—Ç –ò–¥–µ—è –¥–æ MVP)

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –í–∑–∏–º–∞ –≤–∞—à–∞ —Å—É—Ä–æ–≤–∞, –Ω–µ—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∞ –∏–¥–µ—è –∏ —è –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞ –≤ —è—Å–µ–Ω, –µ–¥–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ.
*   –ò–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞ –∫–ª—é—á–æ–≤–∏—Ç–µ –µ–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏, –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º–∏ –∑–∞ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ: MVP (–ú–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª–Ω–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–µ—â –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç), –Ω—É–∂–Ω–∏ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–∏ –∏ –Ω–∞–π-–≤–∞–∂–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ –º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏–∫–∞ –∑–∞ —É—Å–ø–µ—Ö.
*   –ü—Ä–µ–æ–¥–æ–ª—è–≤–∞ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ç–∞ –æ—Ç –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –¥–µ—Ñ–∏–Ω–∏—Ä–∞ –ø—ä—Ä–≤–∏—Ç–µ –ø–µ—Ç –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–∏ —Å—Ç—ä–ø–∫–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ —Ç—Ä—è–±–≤–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø—Ä–∏–µ–º–∞—Ç –≤ —Å–ª–µ–¥–≤–∞—â–∏—Ç–µ 48 —á–∞—Å–∞, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–µ —Å—ä–∑–¥–∞–¥–µ –∏–Ω–µ—Ä—Ü–∏—è.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ù–µ —Å–µ —Ü–µ–Ω–∑—É—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ, –∫–æ–≥–∞—Ç–æ –æ–ø–∏—Å–≤–∞—Ç–µ –∏–¥–µ—è—Ç–∞ —Å–∏. –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ —è –∏–∑–ª–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ —Ç–∞–∫–∞, –∫–∞–∫—Ç–æ –µ –≤ –≥–ª–∞–≤–∞—Ç–∞ –≤–∏.
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∏ –∑–∞ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–∏—Ç–µ, —Å –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–∑–ø–æ–ª–∞–≥–∞—Ç–µ –≤ –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞.
*   –§–æ–∫—É—Å—ä—Ç –µ –≤—ä—Ä—Ö—É —Å–∫–æ—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –∏ –≤–∞–ª–∏–¥–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞, –∞ –Ω–µ –≤—ä—Ä—Ö—É —Å—ä–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –ø–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–µ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a seasoned Venture Catalyst and startup advisor. Your superpower is rapidly transforming a raw idea into a clear, actionable blueprint for validation.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a raw idea for a new project, product, or initiative.

YOUR TASK:
Analyze the user's idea and generate a concise, one-page "Initiative Blueprint" in Markdown. The blueprint must contain the following sections:

1.  **The Core Idea (Elevator Pitch):** Refine the user's input into a compelling, one-sentence pitch.
2.  **Problem & Solution:**
    *   **Problem:** Who is the target audience and what specific, painful problem are you solving for them?
    *   **Solution:** How does this idea solve that problem in a unique way?
3.  **The MVP (Minimum Viable Pilot):**
    *   Describe the absolute simplest version of this idea that can be built/tested to prove the core hypothesis. What features are *excluded*?
    *   **Success Hypothesis:** State the core assumption we are testing. (e.g., "We believe [target audience] will be willing to [take action] if we provide [our MVP].")
4.  **Key Resources Required:**
    *   **People:** What key skills are needed? (e.g., "1 developer, 1 marketer").
    *   **Time (Estimate):** How long would the MVP take to build? (e.g., "2 weeks").
    *   **Budget (Estimate):** What is the rough cost? (e.g., "< $500").
5.  **The North Star Metric:** Define the single, most important number that will tell you if the MVP is successful. (e.g., "Number of sign-ups," "Percentage of users completing the core action").
6.  **The First 5 Steps (48-Hour Action Plan):** List five concrete, small, and immediate actions to get started.
    1.  [e.g., "Interview 3 potential users."]
    2.  [e.g., "Sketch the user flow on paper."]
    3.  [e.g., "Create a simple landing page."]
    4.  [e.g., "Identify the core technology needed."]
    5.  [e.g., "Schedule a 30-min kickoff meeting."]

YOUR TONE: Be sharp, concise, and action-oriented. Eliminate fluff.

MY IDEA: [DUMP YOUR RAW IDEA HERE, IN ANY FORMAT]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª–∏—è –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ù–∞ –º—è—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ `[DUMP YOUR RAW IDEA HERE, IN ANY FORMAT]` –∏–∑–ª–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ –∏–¥–µ—è, –±–µ–∑ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∫–æ–ª–∫–æ –µ –Ω–µ–¥–æ–≤—ä—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∞.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–≤—ä—Ä–Ω–µ—Ç–µ —Ö–∞–æ—Å–∞ –≤ —è—Å–Ω–æ—Ç–∞ –∏ –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –ò–¥–µ–∏—Ç–µ —Å–∞ –±–µ–∑–ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–∏ –±–µ–∑ –∏–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ. –í –∏–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –±—ä–¥–µ—â–µ—Ç–æ, —Å–∫–æ—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –µ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–æ. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –µ –º–æ—Å—Ç—ä—Ç –º–µ–∂–¥—É –º–∏—Å—ä–ª—Ç–∞ –∏ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ—Ç–æ, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏—Ç–µ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç—ä–ø –∞–∫—Å–µ–ª–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∏, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞—Ç–µ –∏–¥–µ–∏—Ç–µ —Å–∏ –±—ä—Ä–∑–æ –∏ –µ–≤—Ç–∏–Ω–æ.

### 18. –°–∏–Ω—Ç–µ–∑–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ –û–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–∞ –í—Ä—ä–∑–∫–∞ –∏ –ü–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –†–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç–∏–µ

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –í–∑–∏–º–∞ –Ω–µ—Å–≤—ä—Ä–∑–∞–Ω–∞, —Å—É—Ä–æ–≤–∞ –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–∞ –≤—Ä—ä–∑–∫–∞ –∑–∞ –≤–∞—Å (–æ—Ç 360-–≥—Ä–∞–¥—É—Å–æ–≤–∏ –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∏, –∞–Ω–∫–µ—Ç–∏, –∫–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ä–∏ –æ—Ç –º–µ–Ω–∏–¥–∂—ä—Ä–∞) –∏ —è —Å–∏–Ω—Ç–µ–∑–∏—Ä–∞ –≤ 3-5 —è—Å–Ω–∏, –ø–æ–≤—Ç–∞—Ä—è—â–∏ —Å–µ —Ç–µ–º–∏.
*   –ò–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ "—Å—É–ø–µ—Ä—Å–∏–ª–∏" (–Ω–µ—â–∞, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–¥—ä–ª–∂–∏—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ) –∏ –Ω–∞–π-–≤–∞–∂–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç –∑–∞ —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç–∏–µ, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ —â–µ –∏–º–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–≥–æ–ª—è–º –µ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç –≤—ä—Ä—Ö—É –∫–∞—Ä–∏–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∞ –≤–∏.
*   –ü–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –≤–∏ –¥–∞ —Å—ä–∑–¥–∞–¥–µ—Ç–µ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–µ–Ω, 90-–¥–Ω–µ–≤–µ–Ω –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ –∑–∞ —Ç–∞–∑–∏ –∫–ª—é—á–æ–≤–∞ –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç, –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞–π–∫–∏ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞—Ç–∞ –≤ –≥–æ—Ä–∏–≤–æ –∑–∞ —Ä–∞—Å—Ç–µ–∂.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –∏ –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–µ—Ç–µ –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ –≤—Ä—ä–∑–∫–∞ –≤—ä–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –Ω–∞–π-—Å—É—Ä–æ–≤–∞, –¥–æ—Ä–∏ —Å –ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ–ø–∏—Å–Ω–∏ –≥—Ä–µ—à–∫–∏. –ù–µ —è —Ä–µ–¥–∞–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ.
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –æ—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–∏ –∫—ä–º —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∞. –ü–æ–Ω—è–∫–æ–≥–∞ –Ω–∞–π-—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏–¥–≤–∞—Ç –æ—Ç –Ω–µ–æ—á–∞–∫–≤–∞–Ω–∏ —Ç–µ–º–∏.
*   –°–ø–æ–¥–µ–ª–µ—Ç–µ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø–ª–∞–Ω —Å –≤–∞—à–∏—è –º–µ–Ω–∏–¥–∂—ä—Ä –∏–ª–∏ –º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ—Ä, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç–µ –ø–æ–¥–∫—Ä–µ–ø–∞ –∏ –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a professional Executive Coach specializing in leadership development and 360-degree feedback analysis. Your task is to process raw, unstructured feedback about me and transform it into a clear, actionable development plan.

CONTEXT: I will paste a collection of raw feedback I have received from peers, direct reports, and my manager.

YOUR TASK:
Think step-by-step to analyze the feedback and create a "Personal Leadership Development Plan":

1.  **Synthesize Key Themes:** Read all the feedback and cluster the comments into 3-5 recurring themes. For each theme, give it a clear name. Separate themes into two categories:
    *   **Strengths ("Superpowers"):** Themes that highlight what you do well and should continue to leverage.
    *   **Areas for Growth:** Themes that point to areas for development.
2.  **Identify the "One Thing":** Based on the "Areas for Growth," identify the single most impactful theme to focus on for the next 90 days. Justify your choice by explaining how improving this one area will create a ripple effect of positive change.
3.  **Craft a 90-Day Development Sprint:** For the chosen "One Thing," create a concrete action plan with the following components:
    *   **Development Goal:** A specific, measurable goal. (e.g., "Improve clarity in team communication by reducing misunderstandings by 50%").
    *   **Key Actions (3-5 items):** Specific behaviors to start, stop, or continue. (e.g., "Start: Send a summary email after every important meeting," "Stop: Making decisions without explaining the 'why'").
    *   **Learning Resources:** Suggest one book, one podcast/video, and one person to talk to for advice on this topic.
    *   **Measurement of Success:** How will you know you've made progress in 90 days? (e.g., "Actively solicit feedback from 3 team members at the end of the quarter").

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use professional and encouraging language. Structure the output in clear Markdown with bold headings for each section.

RAW FEEDBACK: [PASTE ALL THE UNSTRUCTURED FEEDBACK ABOUT YOU HERE]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –í–∑–µ–º–µ—Ç–µ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç–∞ –æ—Ç —á–µ—Ä–Ω–æ—Ç–æ –ø–æ–ª–µ.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ù–∞ –º—è—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ `[PASTE ALL THE UNSTRUCTURED FEEDBACK...]` –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–µ—Ç–µ —Ü—è–ª–∞—Ç–∞ –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–∞ –≤—Ä—ä–∑–∫–∞, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–µ —Å—ä–±—Ä–∞–ª–∏.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –æ–±–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω —Å–∏–Ω—Ç–µ–∑ –∏ —è—Å–µ–Ω –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ —Å–ª–µ–¥–≤–∞—â–∏—Ç–µ 90 –¥–Ω–∏.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –û–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ –≤—Ä—ä–∑–∫–∞ –µ –ø–æ–¥–∞—Ä—ä–∫, –Ω–æ —á–µ—Å—Ç–æ –µ –æ–ø–∞–∫–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∞ –∑–ª–µ. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –µ –≤–∞—à–∏—è—Ç –ª–∏—á–µ–Ω "–ø—Ä–µ–≤–æ–¥–∞—á", –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞ —à—É–º–∞ –≤ —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞–ª. –í –±—ä–¥–µ—â–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç–∞, —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –∑–∞ –±—ä—Ä–∑–∞ –∞–¥–∞–ø—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è –µ –∫–ª—é—á–æ–≤–∞, –∞ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω –¥–∞ —Å–µ –ø—Ä–µ–æ—Ç–∫—Ä–∏–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–Ω–æ.

### 19. –ö–∞—Ç–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –∑–∞ –ú–µ–∂–¥—É–µ–∫–∏–ø–Ω–æ –°—ä—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ

*   –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –Ω–µ—É—Ç—Ä–∞–ª–µ–Ω —Ñ–∞—Å–∏–ª–∏—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—Ä, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –ø–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ –µ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å –∑–∞ —Å—ä—Ç—Ä—É–¥–Ω–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω–∏ –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª–∏ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä. –ü—Ä–æ–¥–∞–∂–±–∏, –ú–∞—Ä–∫–µ—Ç–∏–Ω–≥, –ü—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç).

*   –°—ä–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞ "–•–∞—Ä—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –ü—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞", –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ —Å–ª—É–∂–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω –∏–∑—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫ –Ω–∞ –∏—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ –∏ –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–≤–Ω—è–≤–∞ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–∏ —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏—Ü–∏ –æ–∫–æ–ª–æ –æ–±—â–∞ —Ü–µ–ª –∏ —è—Å–Ω–∏ –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–∏ –∑–∞ —Å—ä—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É–≤–∞—â–∏—Ç–µ "–≤—Ä–∞–∂–¥–∏" –∏–ª–∏ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∏ –º–µ–∂–¥—É –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç–µ. AI —â–µ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–∏ –ø–æ-–∞–¥–µ–∫–≤–∞—Ç–Ω–∏ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è.
*   –í–∫–ª—é—á–µ—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª–∏ –æ—Ç –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–∏ –µ–∫–∏–ø–∏ –≤ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å–∞ –Ω–∞ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ —Ç–∞–∑–∏ —Ö–∞—Ä—Ç–∞.
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ –≥–æ–ª—è–º, –º–µ–∂–¥—É–µ–∫–∏–ø–µ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an expert Agile Coach and organizational designer, specializing in breaking down silos and fostering high-impact cross-functional collaboration.

CONTEXT: The user will describe a project that requires collaboration between multiple teams/departments and will list the teams involved.

YOUR TASK:
Generate a "Cross-Functional Project Charter" designed to align all teams and prevent common friction points. The charter must include:

1.  **The Shared Mission:** Write a single, inspiring sentence that defines the collective goal, transcending individual team objectives.
2.  **Roles & Contributions (RACI-Lite):** Create a table outlining the primary role of each team:
    *   **Team:** [e.g., Marketing, Sales, Product, Engineering]
    *   **Primary Contribution:** What is their unique value-add to this project?
    *   **Accountable For:** What specific outcome is this team ultimately responsible for delivering?
3.  **Anticipated Friction Points:** Based on the typical dynamics between the specified teams, identify the 3 most likely sources of conflict or misunderstanding. For each, describe it clearly. (e.g., "Friction Point 1: Sales promising features that Engineering hasn't built.")
4.  **The Collaboration Compact (Rules of Engagement):** Propose a simple set of 4-5 ground rules for how the teams will work together.
    *   **Communication:** "We will have one central Slack channel for all project updates."
    *   **Decision-Making:** "Decisions affecting multiple teams will be made in the weekly sync, not 1-on-1."
    *   **Conflict Resolution:** "When disagreements arise, we will use the 'Disagree and Commit' principle."
    *   **Defining Success:** "We agree to track our progress against the shared North Star Metric, not just our individual team KPIs."
5.  **Kick-off Meeting Agenda:** Outline a 45-minute agenda for a project kick-off meeting designed to introduce and ratify this charter with all stakeholders.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use clear, structured Markdown. The tone should be neutral, proactive, and facilitative.

PROJECT GOAL: [Describe the goal of the cross-functional initiative.]
TEAMS INVOLVED: [List the departments/teams, e.g., "Marketing, Sales, Product, Engineering"]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**

2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –û–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞ –≤ `[PROJECT GOAL]` –∏ –∏–∑–±—Ä–æ–π—Ç–µ —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–≤–∞—â–∏—Ç–µ –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª–∏ –≤ `[TEAMS INVOLVED]`.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ —â–µ —Å–ø–µ—Å—Ç–∏ —Å–µ–¥–º–∏—Ü–∏ –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Ä–∞–∑—É–º–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏ –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–ª–∏–∫—Ç–∏.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –í —Å—ä–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –Ω–∞–π-–≥–æ–ª—è–º–∞—Ç–∞ –∑–∞–≥—É–±–∞ –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–æ–π–Ω–æ—Å—Ç —Å–µ —Å–ª—É—á–≤–∞ –≤ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ *–º–µ–∂–¥—É* –µ–∫–∏–ø–∏—Ç–µ. –ö–∞—Ç–æ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä, –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ —Ä–æ–ª—è –µ –¥–∞ –±—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ "—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç–µ–ª –Ω–∞ –º–æ—Å—Ç–æ–≤–µ". –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ –∏–Ω–∂–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–Ω–∏—è –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–∂–¥–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —Ç–µ–∑–∏ –º–æ—Å—Ç–æ–≤–µ, –æ—Å–∏–≥—É—Ä—è–≤–∞–π–∫–∏ –ø–ª–∞–≤–µ–Ω –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫ –Ω–∞ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –∏ –µ–Ω–µ—Ä–≥–∏—è.

### 20. –°–∏–º—É–ª–∞—Ç–æ—Ä "–õ–∏—á–µ–Ω –ë–æ—Ä–¥ –Ω–∞ –î–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ"

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –§–æ—Ä–º—É–ª–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–∑–≤–∏–∫–∞—Ç–µ–ª—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ç–æ —Å–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –æ—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω –≤—ä–ø—Ä–æ—Å –∏–ª–∏ –¥–∏–ª–µ–º–∞, –∞ –Ω–µ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤—ä–ø—Ä–æ—Å —Å "–¥–∞/–Ω–µ" –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä.

*   –¢–æ–≤–∞ –µ –Ω–∞–π-–º–æ—â–Ω–∏—è—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –∑–∞ "–º–µ—Ç–∞-–ø–æ–∑–Ω–∞–Ω–∏–µ". –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–≤–∞–∂–Ω–∏—Ç–µ —Å–∏ –∏ —Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω–∏ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as my "Personal Board of Directors." I will present you with a strategic challenge or dilemma I am facing. You will provide feedback from three distinct and powerful personas, one after the other. Do not blend the personas.

Here are your personas:
1.  **The Pragmatic Investor (PI):** You are ruthless, data-driven, and focused solely on ROI, risk, and defensibility. You think in terms of numbers, resources, and competitive moats. Your questions are sharp and skeptical.
2.  **The Customer Advocate (CA):** You are deeply empathetic and obsessed with the customer experience, brand promise, and long-term trust. You think in terms of feelings, stories, and reputation. You ask questions about the "why" and the human impact.
3.  **The Maverick Innovator (MI):** You are a contrarian thinker who challenges the fundamental assumptions of the industry. You think in terms of 10x leaps, not 10% improvements. You ask provocative "What if..." questions to break conventional thinking.

YOUR TASK:
1.  Wait for me to state my strategic challenge.
2.  Respond with three separate paragraphs, clearly labeled **PI:**, **CA:**, and **MI:**.
3.  In each paragraph, embody the corresponding persona and provide one critical question and one piece of direct advice regarding my challenge.

Let's begin.

MY STRATEGIC CHALLENGE: [Clearly and concisely describe the strategic problem, dilemma, or opportunity you are facing.]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**

2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ù–∞ –º—è—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ `[MY STRATEGIC CHALLENGE...]` –æ–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –≤–∞—à–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞–π-–≥–æ–ª—è–º–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–∑–≤–∏–∫–∞—Ç–µ–ª—Å—Ç–≤–æ –≤ –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–µ–∑–∞–±–∞–≤–Ω–∞ –º—ä–¥—Ä–æ—Å—Ç –æ—Ç —Ç—Ä–∏ —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω–∏ –≥–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏ —Ç–æ—á–∫–∏.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –ù–∏–∫–æ–π –Ω–µ –µ –ø–æ-—É–º–µ–Ω –æ—Ç –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–∏. –ù–∞–π-–≥–æ–ª–µ–º–∏—è—Ç —Ä–∏—Å–∫ –∑–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä –µ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ø–∞–¥–Ω–µ –≤ –∫–∞–ø–∞–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ —Å–∏ –≥–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ—á–∫–∞. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –µ –≤–∞—à–µ—Ç–æ "—Ç–∞–π–Ω–æ –æ—Ä—ä–∂–∏–µ" —Å—Ä–µ—â—É "—Å–ª–µ–ø–∏—Ç–µ –ø–µ—Ç–Ω–∞", –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—ä–ø –¥–æ —Ä–∞–∑–Ω–æ–æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–Ω–∞ –µ–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç–∏–∑–∞ –ø–æ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –∏ –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–∞,
—á–µ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–∞–π-–≤–∞–∂–Ω–∏ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å–∞ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞–Ω–∏ –ø–æ–¥ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–µ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ.

### 21. –ê—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç –∑–∞ –†–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –¢–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Ç–∏

*   –ó–∞–º–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –æ–±—â–∏—Ç–µ HR —à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω–∏ —Å –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–µ–Ω, –º–æ—Ç–∏–≤–∏—Ä–∞—â –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –ø–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –∑–∞ –∑–∞–¥—ä—Ä–∂–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ–ø —Ç–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Ç–∏.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–∏ –∏ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–∏ –æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å–Ω–æ —Å–∏–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏ –∏ –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –∑–∞ —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç–∏–µ –Ω–∞ —Å–ª—É–∂–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è.
*   –í–∫–ª—é—á–µ—Ç–µ —Å–ª—É–∂–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è –≤ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å–∞ ‚Äì –ø–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ –≤—Ö–æ–¥–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏ –∑–∞–µ–¥–Ω–æ –∏–ª–∏ –æ–±—Å—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∫–∞—Ç–æ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ—á–∫–∞.
*   –ù–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∏ —Å **GPT-4o** –∑–∞—Ä–∞–¥–∏ —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –º—É –¥–∞ —Ä–∞–∑–±–∏—Ä–∞ –Ω—é–∞–Ω—Å–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ —á–æ–≤–µ—à–∫–∏—è –ø–æ—Ç–µ–Ω—Ü–∏–∞–ª –∏ –∫–æ—Ä–ø–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∞—Ç–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—è.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an Executive Talent Development Coach from a top-tier consulting firm like Korn Ferry. Your task is to create a structured, inspiring, and actionable 6-month "Growth & Impact Plan" for one of my team members.

CONTEXT: I will provide you with the team member's role, their key strengths, areas for growth, and their long-term aspirations.

YOUR TASK:
Analyze the input and generate the plan using the following structure:

1.  **The North Star (Future Role Aspiration):** Based on their aspirations, define a compelling "future self" vision. (e.g., "Evolving from a Senior Developer into a Tech Lead and Systems Architect.")
2.  **The Impact Project (The "Stretch" Assignment):** Propose one significant project or responsibility for the next 6 months that directly aligns with their growth areas and the team's goals. This should be a challenging but achievable assignment.
3.  **Core Competency Focus (Skill Development):** Identify the top 2 skills they need to develop to succeed in the Impact Project and their North Star role.
4.  **Actionable Development Plan (The "How"):** Create a table with three columns for the two focus skills:
    *   **Skill:** [e.g., "Stakeholder Communication"]
    *   **Experience (70%):** How can they practice this skill on the job? (e.g., "Lead the weekly update meeting for the project.")
    *   **Exposure (20%):** Who can they learn from? (e.g., "Shadow Sarah during a client negotiation.")
    *   **Education (10%):** What formal learning can help? (e.g., "Complete the online course on 'Crucial Conversations'.")
5.  **Measuring Success (The Proof):** Define 2-3 clear, measurable outcomes that will indicate success at the end of the 6 months. (e.g., "Successfully delivered the Impact Project on time," "Received positive feedback from 3 stakeholders on communication clarity.")

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use professional, encouraging language. Structure the output as a clean Markdown document titled "Growth & Impact Plan for [Employee Name]".

EMPLOYEE'S NAME: [Enter name]
CURRENT ROLE: [Enter role]
KEY STRENGTHS: [List 2-3 key strengths]
AREAS FOR GROWTH: [List 1-2 critical areas for development]
LONG-TERM ASPIRATIONS: [Describe their career goals as you understand them]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª–∏—è –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç –æ—Ç–≥–æ—Ä–µ.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –∑–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—è —Å–ª—É–∂–∏—Ç–µ–ª –≤ –ø–µ—Ç—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–Ω–ª–∏–≤–∏ –≤ –∫—Ä–∞—è.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤ –ø–ª–∞–Ω, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –¥–∞ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Å–ª–µ–¥–≤–∞—â–∏—è –≤–∏ 1-–Ω–∞-1 —Ä–∞–∑–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä –Ω–∞–π-—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞ –≥–æ–¥–∏–Ω–∞—Ç–∞.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –í –∏–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ 2025-2030, —Ö–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏–∏, –∞ –º–µ–Ω–∏–¥–∂—ä—Ä–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –∏–Ω–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä–∞—Ç –≤ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏—è —Ä–∞—Å—Ç–µ–∂. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä—ä—â–∞ –≤ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–∂–¥–∞ —Ç–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Ç–∏, —Å—ä–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞–π–∫–∏ –ª–æ—è–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç –∏ –µ–∫–∏–ø, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–µ –¥–∞ –ø–æ—Å—Ä–µ—â–Ω–µ –±—ä–¥–µ—â–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–∑–≤–∏–∫–∞—Ç–µ–ª—Å—Ç–≤–∞.

### 22. –°—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥ –∑–∞ –ü—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Ç–≤—Ä–∞—Ç—è–≤–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ "–ë—ä—Ä–Ω–∞—É—Ç"

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –ò–∑–≤—ä—Ä—à–≤–∞ "–û–¥–∏—Ç –Ω–∞ –£—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞" –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—è –µ–∫–∏–ø, –∫–∞—Ç–æ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å–∏, –Ω–∞—Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–≤–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –∏ –∫—É–ª—Ç—É—Ä–∞—Ç–∞ –∑–∞ —Å–∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏ —Ä–∏—Å–∫–æ–≤–µ –æ—Ç –ø—Ä–µ–≥–∞—Ä—è–Ω–µ (–±—ä—Ä–Ω–∞—É—Ç).
*   –ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ –Ω–∞ —Ç—Ä–∏ –Ω–∏–≤–∞ (—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω–æ, –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å–∫–æ, –µ–∫–∏–ø–Ω–æ), –∑–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–µ —Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ —Å –ø—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω–∏—Ç–µ, –∞ –Ω–µ —Å—ä—Å —Å–∏–º–ø—Ç–æ–º–∏—Ç–µ –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–µ—Å–∞.
*   –ó–∞–º–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –±–µ–∑–ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–∏—Ç–µ "—É–µ–ª–Ω–µ—Å" –∏–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞—Ç–∏–≤–∏ (–∫–∞—Ç–æ –π–æ–≥–∞ –≤ –æ—Ñ–∏—Å–∞) —Å —Ä–µ–∞–ª–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –≤ –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –ø–æ–¥–æ–±—Ä—è–≤–∞—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ –∏ –±–ª–∞–≥–æ—Å—ä—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ—Ç–æ.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª–Ω–æ —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–∏ –∏ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–∏ –≤ –æ–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞–ª–∏—Ç–µ –∑–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–µ—Å. –ö–æ–ª–∫–æ—Ç–æ –ø–æ–≤–µ—á–µ –¥–µ—Ç–∞–π–ª–∏, —Ç–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤–∞ –ø–æ-—Ç–æ—á–µ–Ω –µ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑—ä—Ç.
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∏ –¥–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å–∏, –∞ –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –¥–∞ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤—è—Ç–µ "–ø–µ—Ä–∫–∏". –ò—Å—Ç–∏–Ω—Å–∫–∏—Ç–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è —á–µ—Å—Ç–æ —Å–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–Ω–∏.
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞ –∑–∞ –æ—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω —Ä–∞–∑–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä —Å –µ–∫–∏–ø–∞ —Å–∏.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an Organizational Psychologist specializing in team resilience and burnout prevention. Your task is to conduct a "Team Resilience Audit" based on my observations and design a proactive intervention plan.

CONTEXT: I will describe my team, their current workload and context, and any signals of stress or potential burnout I've noticed.

YOUR TASK:
Analyze my input against the six primary scientifically-validated causes of burnout (Workload, Control, Reward, Community, Fairness, Values). Then, generate a "Team Resilience Action Plan" with the following structure:

1.  **Primary Burnout Risk Factors:** Based on my description, identify the top 2-3 most likely root causes of stress for my team. For each, briefly explain your reasoning. (e.g., "Risk 1: Lack of Control - The team feels micromanaged and unable to influence project deadlines.")
2.  **The Intervention Plan (A 3-Tiered Approach):**
    *   **Tier 1: Systemic & Process Changes:** Recommend 1-2 specific changes to the *way* work is done to address the root causes. (e.g., "Implement 'no-meeting Fridays' to create dedicated focus time," "Introduce a clearer project intake process to manage workload.")
    *   **Tier 2: Leadership Behaviors:** Suggest 1-2 specific behaviors that *I*, as the leader, should start or stop doing. (e.g., "Start: Publicly acknowledge and celebrate small wins and effort, not just outcomes," "Stop: Sending non-urgent emails or Slack messages after work hours.")
    *   **Tier 3: Team Rituals:** Propose 1-2 simple, collective habits the team can build together to foster community and psychological safety. (e.g., "Begin the weekly team meeting with a 5-minute 'check-in' on personal energy levels," "Create a dedicated Slack channel for sharing non-work-related successes.")
3.  **Leading Indicators of Success:** How will we know the plan is working? List 2-3 observable, positive changes to look for in the next 30-60 days. (e.g., "Increased proactive communication from team members," "Fewer tasks slipping past deadlines due to overload.")

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use a structured, empathetic, and professional tone. Use Markdown for clarity and readability.

TEAM DESCRIPTION & CONTEXT: [Describe your team, its size, and what it does.]
CURRENT WORKLOAD & PRESSURES: [e.g., "We are in a pre-launch phase, working long hours. There is high pressure from leadership."]
OBSERVED STRESS SIGNALS: [e.g., "I've noticed increased cynicism in meetings, more sick days, simple mistakes being made, people being quiet."]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏—è —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç –æ—Ç –∫–æ–¥–∞.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ —Ç—Ä–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–Ω–ª–∏–≤–∏ —Å —á–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–∞ –æ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ —Å–∏—Ç—É–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ –≤—ä–≤ –≤–∞—à–∏—è –µ–∫–∏–ø.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –µ–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç–µ–Ω –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–∂–¥–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –ø–æ-–∑–¥—Ä–∞–≤ –∏ –ø–æ-—É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤ –µ–∫–∏–ø.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –í –µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ "–ø–µ—Ä–º–∞–∫—Ä–∏–∑–∞", –±—ä—Ä–Ω–∞—É—Ç—ä—Ç –Ω–µ –µ –ª–∏—á–µ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª, –∞ –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–µ–Ω –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º. –ï–∫–∏–ø–∏—Ç–µ, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ —Å–∞ —É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–∏, –∞ –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –∑–∞–µ—Ç–∏, —â–µ –±—ä–¥–∞—Ç —Ç–µ–∑–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –ø–µ—á–µ–ª—è—Ç. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–¥–∏—Ç–µ "–∞–Ω—Ç–∏-–∫—Ä–µ—Ö—ä–∫" –µ–∫–∏–ø, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü—ä—Ñ—Ç—è–≤–∞ –ø–æ–¥ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–µ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ.
